| 0:03:17| As our thoughts and prayers have gone out to all of those communities, people here and across the country are feeling hurt and angry, sorrowful, and afraid.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=197)|

| 1:45:56| Let me start with some background in the program and some of the rationale for how the program works.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6356)|
| 1:46:05| I'm sure you've all heard this before, but just so that we're all on the same page, some background is sometimes useful.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6365)|
| 1:46:12| Federal Emergency Management Agency provides insurance to property owners through the National Flood Insurance Program.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6372)|
| 1:46:21| Flood insurance provides resources for rebuilding communities when a flood occurs.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6381)|
| 1:46:27| If there is no flood insurance, there are no outside resources that come in.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6387)|
| 1:46:32| Non-participating communities do not get support to rebuild a community that's been flooded.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6392)|
| 1:46:40| The Flood Insurance Program is also structured to encourage communities to reduce the amount of rebuilding that would be required when that flood happens.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6400)|
| 1:46:51| One way to meet this goal of reducing the amount of rebuilding is to prevent significant investment in non-compliant, flood-prone structures.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6411)|
| 1:47:03| The basic FEMA requirements must be met in order for a community to participate in the Flood Insurance Program,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6423)|
| 1:47:12| but FEMA also has an additional program called the Community Rating System that provides an opportunity for communities to go beyond that minimum| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6432)|
| 1:47:24| and get discounts on their insurance rates.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6444)|
| 1:47:29| The best rating is a 1. The basic minimum compliance is a 10.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6449)|
| 1:47:39| We currently have an 8.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6459)|
| 1:47:43| A better rating is attained through policies, regulations, and practices that go beyond the minimum that FEMA requires.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6463)|
| 1:47:52| Along with those policies is consistent application of those policies.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6472)|
| 1:47:57| That's really important to maintaining your CRS score.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6477)|
| 1:48:04| We're at an 8.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=6484)|

| 2:14:04| I especially want to thank Mark Mamentoff and both he and Allison Dyer for their help.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8044)|
| 2:14:09| Allison is here this evening, and she's an attorney for the city of Knoxville.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8049)|
| 2:14:13| I hate to read this, but I am going to kind of read this because there are a lot of details,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8053)|
| 2:14:18| and I just want to make sure I don't forget anything that's important for you guys to know.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8058)|
| 2:14:22| So we'll start with a brief background because it's been a few months.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8062)|
| 2:14:26| On October 15, 2015, the city and Regal Cinemas, with the help of KCDC and IDB,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8066)|
| 2:14:31| entered into a letter of intent committing each party to working on the redevelopment of a site| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8071)|
| 2:14:37| in an area previously known as Baptist Hospital of East Tennessee.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8077)|
| 2:14:41| The objective of this work has been to lease the property at 101 East Blount Avenue to Regal Cinemas| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8081)|
| 2:14:46| as a corporate headquarters with the intent of promoting high-quality employment in the downtown area| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8086)|
| 2:14:51| and assisting with the overall redevelopment of the Baptist Hospital site.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8091)|
| 2:14:55| CETA had purchased the full 23-acre site from Tenova, which was Baptist Hospital's successor,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8095)|
| 2:15:00| and they did that in 2013, to redevelop the site as a mixed-use development of luxury apartments,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8100)|
| 2:15:06| student housing, hotel, retail shopping, and restaurants and public spaces,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8106)|
| 2:15:10| including a riverwalk, a park, and an entertainment plaza.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8110)|
| 2:15:14| A TIF district was established to support CETA's project.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8114)|
| 2:15:18| The building that we're talking about is located at the corner of Gay Street and Blount Avenue.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8118)|
| 2:15:23| It's nine stories and 178,000 square feet.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8123)|
| 2:15:26| The building is 26 years old, and it's been vacant since 2008, so several years now,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8126)|
| 2:15:31| and as you can imagine, it needs a lot of work for it to function appropriately for Regal's needs.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8131)|
| 2:15:36| The basic concept of the deal is this.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8136)|
| 2:15:38| IDB will purchase this nine-story building from Southeastern Development Associates.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8138)|
| 2:15:43| You guys may recall that Southeastern Development Associates, also known as CETA,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8143)|
| 2:15:47| is the successor organization to Blanchard Calhoun.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8147)|
| 2:15:51| This means that the building will be removed from the south waterfront TIF district.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8151)|
| 2:15:56| The IDB will then lease the building to Regal Cinemas on a triple-net basis,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8156)|
| 2:16:00| which means Regal will be responsible for all taxes, insurance, maintenance, utilities, everything.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8160)|
| 2:16:06| The building will be renovated by Regal at their cost with some tenant improvement contributions| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8166)|
| 2:16:10| coming from CETA, the city of Knoxville, Knox County, and the state of Tennessee.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8170)|
| 2:16:16| TVA will contribute also with a utility asset improvement grant.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8176)|
| 2:16:20| Funds have been transferred from the city to the IDB.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8180)|
| 2:16:23| The county has allocated their funding.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8183)|
| 2:16:25| CETA's contribution will be made pursuant to the terms of a purchase and sell agreement,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8185)|
| 2:16:30| and the state's grant money will be distributed pursuant to a reimbursement plan.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8190)|
| 2:16:35| Again, these funds will be used by the IDB to purchase the building| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8195)|
| 2:16:38| and for contributions towards some of the tenant improvement work.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8198)|
| 2:16:42| The initial lease term is 10 years with two successive option terms of 10 years each.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8202)|
| 2:16:47| As long as the lease is in effect, Regal shall have the option to purchase the building for $9 million,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncil160719?start=8207)|
